### [290] [SUDA-Muon: Structural Design Principles and Boundaries for Fully Decentralized Muon](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23980)
*Hengrui Zhang,Boao Kong,Jiahe Geng,Zhengyang Huang*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为SUDA的统一原始-对偶通信模板，用于实现去中心化Muon优化器。该模板将去中心化Muon的设计问题分解为模块化的通信骨干（如ED/D²、EXTRA、梯度跟踪）和非模块化的极化操作。理论上证明了在核范数几何下拓扑分离的收敛保证，并识别了内部和外部两个非模块化边界。实验表明，在非IID设置下，基于SUDA的SudAMuon优于DeMuon。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 去中心化Muon由于非线性矩阵符号算符与线性gossip平均不交换，导致算法设计困难。现有方法无法清晰区分模块化组件与非模块化组件，缺乏统一的设计模板，使得不同通信算法的比较和分析混乱。

Method: 提出SUDA（统一原始-对偶通信模板），将去中心化Muon分解为模块化通信骨干（ED/D²、EXTRA、梯度跟踪等）和非模块化本地极化操作。通过拓扑分离的收敛分析，证明主导项为O((1+σ/√N)K^{-1/4})，不显式依赖图拓扑。识别两个非模块化边界：内部边界要求跟踪-先于-极化以避免异构目标下的非平稳不动点；外部边界证明本地极化-再-平均设计是缺乏线性加速的根本原因。

Result: 理论结果表明主导收敛项不显式包含图拓扑量，将通信骨干识别为结构设计的模块化轴。实验上，在CIFAR-100和GPT-2微调中，统一模板使不同通信算法可直接比较；在近IID场景下各变体表现相似，而在长期非IID的CIFAR-100设置中，SudAMuon比DeMuon实现了更高准确率和更低损失。

Conclusion: 去中心化Muon的设计关键在于区分模块化组件（通信骨干）与非模块化组件（极化操作）。SUDA模板成功实现了这一分离，提供了理论保证和实验验证。这为去中心化优化器的结构化设计提供了新范式。

Abstract: Fully decentralized Muon is difficult because its nonlinear matrix-sign operator does not commute with linear gossip averaging. This makes decentralized Muon a structural design problem: in designing the algorithm, one must distinguish modular components from non-modular ones. We propose \sudamuon{}, which realizes this separation through a unified primal--dual communication template called SUDA; within this template, ED/D$^2$, EXTRA, and gradient tracking become modular backbone choices. We prove a topology-separated non-asymptotic convergence guarantee in the nuclear-norm geometry: the dominant term scales as $\mathcal{O}((1+σ/\sqrt{N})K^{-1/4})$ and does not explicitly involve graph quantities, identifying the communication backbone as the modular axis in the structure design. We then establish two complementary non-modular boundaries. Internally, tracking-before-polarization is necessary for this natural no-tracking variant to avoid non-stationary fixed points under heterogeneous objectives. Externally, in the absence of a central server, a fully decentralized method cannot perform the federated average-then-polarize update; we show that this non-modular local-polarize-then-average design is the essential reason why can fail to exhibit linear speedup. Experiments on CIFAR-100 and GPT-2 fine-tuning support the same picture: the unified template makes different communication algorithms directly comparable. In mild near-IID regimes, the resulting variants perform similarly, while in the more difficult long-horizon non-IID CIFAR-100 setting, \sudamuon{} achieves higher accuracy and lower loss than \textsc{DeMuon}.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决连续边际最优传输问题，即给定时间连续的概率边际族，恢复最小能量速度场，该问题是经典Benamou-Brenier公式的连续极限，也是Nelson随机最优传输问题的确定性极限。

We propose a practical mesh-free solver for this problem. The weak continuity equation is embedded in a reproducing kernel Hilbert space, yielding a sample-only objective that requires no spatial discretization. The velocity is parametrized by any linear-in-parameters dictionary or neural network, and is optimized by mini-batch stochastic methods. Synthetic experiments confirm that the method achieves accurate drift recovery and marginal consistency. The same computational framework also applies to the stochastic Nelson problem.

Abstract: This paper studies economic model predictive Control (EMPC) schemes, where the stage cost depends only on control inputs. We show that, under a strict dissipativity assumption related to the set of optimal steady states, the closed-loop trajectories converge asymptotically to this set, ensuring convergence of the economic cost to the optimal steady state cost. To enhance Lyapunov stability, we propose a modified stage cost that preserves the optimal input while guaranteeing asymptotic stability of a specific equilibrium with a slight performance loss. The approach is further extended to EMPC of a class of linear systems with periodic costs and disturbances by lifting it to a multi-step EMPC problem for periodic operations. A case study with a water distribution network demonstrates the effectiveness of the proposed methods in achieving both asymptotic convergence and stability.

Method: 基于Agrachev和Sarychev提出的几何控制方法进行适应性调整，通过二维控制输入实现近似可控性。对于随机强迫方程，采用非退化且统计周期性的随机力进行分析。

Result: 证明了环面上非线性Benjamin-Ono方程在二维控制输入下具有L^2近似可控性；对于随机强迫方程，证明了轨迹在Sobolev范数下几乎必然无界。

Conclusion: 几何控制方法可有效推广至Benjamin-Ono方程，且随机强迫下的无界性结果揭示了该系统的复杂动力学行为。

Abstract: We establish the approximate controllability in $L^2$ for the nonlinear Benjamin-Ono equation on torus via two-dimensional control input. Our proof is based on adaptations of geometric control approach introduced by Agrachev and Sarychev. As an application of this control result, we study long-time dynamics of a randomly forced equation. It is proved that the trajectories are unbounded in Sobolev norms almost surely, when the random force is nondegenerate and statistically periodic in time.

</details>


### [296] [Heterogeneous-Horizon Exact-Weight Local SGD](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24463)
*Dmitry Pasechnyuk-Vilensky,Martin Takáč,Eduard Gorbunov*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 本文针对凸有限和优化中的异构局部SGD问题，提出了HEW-Local SGD方法，通过最小化显式单轮上界自适应选择服务器权重，实现了异构本地轮数、小批量大小、梯度噪声和参与率下的精确局部控制，并提供了单步保障与全局收敛性分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有局部SGD方法通常假设同构设置（如相同本地轮数），但实际中节点计算能力和数据分布存在异构性。本文旨在解决异构局部SGD的自适应聚合问题，提供理论保证的同时匹配现有方法的通信效率。

Method: 提出HEW-Local SGD方法：通过最小化下一目标值的显式单轮上界来确定每个节点的服务器权重，形成一个阈值单纯形更新与可分离幅度更新。同时引入两种后局部变体：修正的异构方法和更简单的同构特例。

Result: 建立了单步保障和全局基准风格收敛结果。在可比条件下，理论结果在定性上匹配现有LocalSGD/SCAFFOLD分析的通信效率图像，同时为不等本地轮数提供了显式保障。

Conclusion: HEW-Local SGD通过自适应权重选择有效处理了异构局部SGD中的多种异质性来源，提供了严格的理论保证，拓展了局部SGD方法在异构场景下的适用性。

Abstract: We study adaptive aggregation for heterogeneous local SGD in convex finite-sum optimization, allowing heterogeneous local horizons, minibatch sizes, gradient noise, and participation. We introduce HEW-Local SGD, a corrected local-SGD method that chooses nodewise server weights by minimizing an explicit one-round upper bound on the next objective value. This yields an exact local-control formulation with a threshold simplex update, separable amplitude updates, and a one-step guarantee under arbitrary predictable participation. We also introduce two post-local variants: a corrected heterogeneous method and a simpler homogeneous specialization. We establish one-step guarantees and global benchmark-style convergence results. In the regimes where comparison is appropriate, the theory matches the qualitative communication-efficient picture of recent LocalSGD/SCAFFOLD analyses, while also giving explicit guarantees for unequal local horizons.

### [297] [Scheduling and Routing in the Flexible Job Shop with Heterogeneous Transbots and Zoning: A Constraint Programming Approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24483)
*Arnovi Moinuddin,El Mehdi Er Raqabi,Pascal Van Hentenryck*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 本文针对配备异构移动运输机器人（transbot）的柔性作业车间问题，提出两种约束规划模型（弧模型与操作嵌入模型），结合分区约束、跨区交接与无碰撞路径规划，并设计了一种"预订-释放"策略来协调运输任务，通过计算实验验证了方法的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代制造系统中移动运输机器人的使用日益普及，但现有研究对异构机器人、分区约束和跨区交接等实际因素的整合不足，导致生产调度与物料运输之间的协调问题计算复杂度高，亟需高效求解方法。

Method: 提出两种约束规划（CP）公式：弧公式显式建模机器间转移，操作嵌入公式将转移决策嵌入操作调度结构实现更紧的同步；设计预订-释放策略协调机器人运动；基于实际案例改编的基准实例进行实验验证。

Result: 所提公式在改编的基准实例上生成了高质量解，表现出强计算性能；详细的实例生成方法为后续研究提供了支持。

Conclusion: 集成生产调度与机器人路径规划的约束规划方法能有效处理异构机器人、分区约束和跨区交接带来的复杂性，预订-释放策略在避免刚性路径模式的同时实现了高效协调。

Abstract: Coordinating production and material transfers is increasingly important in modern manufacturing systems equipped with mobile transfer robots, known as transbots. This study considers a flexible job shop environment in which heterogeneous transbots transport parts between machines. The shop floor is partitioned into zones, with each transbot assigned to a specific zone, and inter-zone movements are facilitated through designated handoff points. These zoning constraints, transbot heterogeneity, and inter-zone handoffs give rise to a challenging variant of the flexible job shop problem with embedded transbot-routing features, resulting in substantial computational complexity. Motivated by a real manufacturing setting, two constraint programming formulations that integrate production scheduling with transbot routing are proposed: an arc-based formulation that explicitly models machine-to-machine transfers, and an operation-embedded formulation that embeds transfer decisions directly within the operation scheduling structure, leading to tighter synchronization between production and transportation decisions. Both formulations capture machine flexibility, zoning restrictions, handoff coordination, and collision-free path planning. To efficiently solve the resulting problem, a book-and-release strategy is proposed. It coordinates transbot movements without enforcing rigid routing patterns. Computational experiments on case study-adapted benchmark-based demonstrate that the proposed formulations generate high-quality solutions with strong computational performance. The generation of instances is described in detail to support future work in this emerging area.

</details>


### [298] [PRP, HS and LS Conjugate Gradient Methods for Interval-Valued Multiobjective Optimization Problems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24605)
*Tapas Mondal,Debdulal Ghosh,Zai-Yun Peng,Yong Zhao*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 本文开发了基于三种非线性共轭梯度法变体（PRP、HS、LS）的高效算法，用于求解无约束区间值多目标优化问题的Pareto临界点。算法采用Wolfe线搜索策略，证明了全局收敛性，并通过数值实验和性能分析验证了有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对无约束区间值多目标优化问题中计算Pareto临界点的需求，现有方法效率不足，需要开发更高效的算法。

Method: 提出三种基于非线性共轭梯度法（PRP、HS、LS变体）的算法，结合Wolfe线搜索策略确定步长，并建立全局收敛性理论分析。

Result: 在基准测试问题上进行数值实验，并通过性能分析证明了所提方法的有效性。

Conclusion: 所提出的三种非线性共轭梯度法变体在求解区间值多目标优化Pareto临界点问题上具有全局收敛性和良好的数值表现。

Abstract: In this article, we develop an efficient algorithm based on three special variants of the nonlinear conjugate gradient method, namely, the Polak--Ribiere--Polyak, Hestenes--Stiefel, and Liu--Story schemes for computing Pareto critical points in unconstrained interval-valued multiobjective optimization problems. The proposed algorithm incorporates a Wolfe line search strategy to determine a suitable range of step size that satisfies the standard Wolfe conditions. For each of the proposed variants of the nonlinear conjugate gradient method, we establish rigorous global convergence results under appropriate assumptions. To demonstrate the effectiveness of the proposed methods, we conduct numerical experiments on a set of benchmark test problems and present a comprehensive performance profile analysis.

### [299] [Dual Control of Linear Systems from Bilinear Observations with Belief Space Model Predictive Control](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24663)
*Daniel Cao,Beixi Du,Andrew Lowitt,Sunmook Choi,Sarah Dean,Yahya Sattar*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 本文针对具有双线性观测的线性系统有限时域二次控制问题，提出了一种信念空间模型预测控制（B-MPC）方法，该方法通过输入依赖卡尔曼滤波器直接规划状态估计及其误差协方差，数值实验表明其在估计协方差和不确定性感知方面优于分离原则控制器。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在具有双线性观测的线性系统中，控制输入不仅影响状态动态，还影响状态的部分观测，导致分离原则失效，因为控制输入会影响未来状态估计的质量。

Method: 提出信念空间模型预测控制（B-MPC），利用输入依赖卡尔曼滤波器构建信念演化的确定性代理，直接在估计状态及其误差协方差上进行规划。

Result: 在两种合成场景的数值实验中，B-MPC在有利条件下优于分离原则控制器及其MPC变体，同时表现出更低的估计协方差和更具备不确定性感知的行动选择。

Conclusion: B-MPC通过显式建模控制输入对状态估计质量的影响，能够获得比传统分离原则方法更好的控制性能。

Abstract: We study finite-horizon quadratic control of linear systems with bilinear observations, in which the control input affects not only the state dynamics but also the partial observations of the state. In this setting, the separation principle can fail because control inputs influence the future quality of state estimates. State estimation requires an input-dependent Kalman filter whose gain and error covariance evolve as functions of the control inputs. To address this challenge, we propose a belief-space model predictive control ($\texttt{B-MPC}$) method that plans directly over both the estimated state and its error covariance. In particular, $\texttt{B-MPC}$ plans with a deterministic surrogate of the belief evolution defined by the input-dependent Kalman filter. Through numerical experiments in two synthetic settings, we show that $\texttt{B-MPC}$ can outperform both the separation-principle controller and its MPC variant in favorable regimes, and that these gains are accompanied by lower estimation covariance and more uncertainty-aware action choices.

</details>
